# Completed Tasks

- [x] AND-20260414-H3. `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/ui/navigation/AppNavGraph.kt` ‚Äî the `Screen.TicketDetail` composable was calling `TicketDetailScreen(...)` without supplying `onNavigateToInvoice`, so the default no-op ran. `TicketDetailViewModel.convertToInvoice()` already sets `convertedInvoiceId` on a successful `POST /tickets/:id/convert-to-invoice` response, and the screen's `LaunchedEffect(state.convertedInvoiceId)` already calls `onNavigateToInvoice(id)` + `clearConvertedInvoiceId()` ‚Äî the only missing wire was the callback itself. Passed `onNavigateToInvoice = { id -> navController.navigate(Screen.InvoiceDetail.createRoute(id)) }` into the call site so a successful Convert-to-Invoice now lands on the new `Screen.InvoiceDetail` route (`invoices/{id}`) where a technician can review or collect payment. Double-submit guard was already in place (`IconButton(onClick = { showConvertConfirm = true }, enabled = !state.isActionInProgress)` at TicketDetailScreen.kt:427-430), so no VM or screen changes were needed ‚Äî the fix is a 4-line nav-graph wire. Verified with `JAVA_HOME=...Android Studio/jbr ./gradlew.bat :app:compileDebugKotlin` ‚Äî BUILD SUCCESSFUL. Commit d8d2cdc.

Per TODO allowance ("If absent: that is acceptable"), left absent ‚Äî especially because git remote is `https://github.com/Sirovensky/BizarreCRM.git` (not the `bizarreelectronics/bizarre-crm` pattern referenced in the task hint), so inventing a URL would be wrong per the TODO's own "Don't invent a URL" rule. No changes. **Smoke test:** ran `cd packages/web && npm run build` ‚Äî completed in 8.41s, produced the full `dist/` tree (41 page chunks + recharts/index/purify/Settings/etc. verified in output). **Audit artefact:** added a "Supply-chain hygiene audits" section to `SECURITY.md` documenting all three findings so future PRs adding `repository`/`bugs`/`homepage` with the wrong URL, absolute paths in scripts, or any lifecycle install hook will trip the on-review checklist. Commit 5cf6151.

- [x] D5-5. `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/ui/screens/pos/CheckoutScreen.kt` ‚Äî two-part fix. **Snackbar spam:** the `LaunchedEffect(state.error)` error handler was re-keying on every `error ‚Üí null ‚Üí error` cycle (state-clear from `clearError()` followed by a fresh network-failure write), and `SnackbarHostState`'s FIFO queue forced the cashier to sit through 15 identical "Network error" toasts rotating off one at a time (~60s of dead UI on a broken Wi-Fi map). Primary debounce was already correctly wired before this task ‚Äî `BrandPrimaryButton(enabled = state.canComplete && !state.isProcessing)` on the CTA + `if (s.isProcessing) return` in `completePayment()` ‚Äî so the spam was purely from stale error states re-firing after each clear, not from unthrottled taps. Added belt-and-suspenders: `snackbarHostState.currentSnackbarData?.dismiss()` immediately before `showSnackbar(it)` so any in-flight toast is superseded rather than queued behind the new message. **Cash-vs-card offline split:** the pre-fix offline branch dispatched ALL `selectedMethod` values ‚Äî including CARD ‚Äî through `completePaymentOffline()` ‚Üí `SyncQueueDao.insert("checkout", operation="convert_and_pay")`. `SyncManager.dispatchCheckoutEntry()` replays the entry once network returns by calling `ticketApi.convertToInvoice(...)` + `invoiceApi.recordPayment(...)`. That's correct for cash (funds are physically in the drawer, queue write is bookkeeping-only) but unrecoverable fraud exposure for card (no BlockChyp round-trip ever captured funds; the cashier could hand goods back on a "successful" local mark). Fix: added a method-discriminator in the offline branch ‚Äî CARD surfaces error "Card payments require an internet connection. Switch to Cash to save offline." and flips `isProcessing=false` without queuing; CASH + OTHER continue to the existing `completePaymentOffline()` path unchanged, preserving the offline-cash-sale happy path through `SyncQueue` + `onSuccess()`. Verified with `./gradlew :app:compileDebugKotlin` ‚Äî BUILD SUCCESSFUL. Commit aa7f23d.

- [x] D5-8. Walked every screen under `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/ui/screens/` for the `OutlinedTextField` / `TextField` + missing-`Modifier.imePadding()` combination. 14 of 19 input-bearing screens already wired `imePadding()` at the Scaffold / outer Column from earlier work; the chat/SMS composer (`SmsThreadScreen.kt`) already had it. The five gaps were all detail screens whose bottom-anchored dialogs and inputs (payment-record amount, stock-adjust quantity, ticket comment composer, part-search price, profile password/PIN change) sat inside a Scaffold whose root `modifier` was unset ‚Äî the soft keyboard ate them instead of the content resizing. Patched `TicketDetailScreen.kt`, `InvoiceDetailScreen.kt`, `ProfileScreen.kt`, `TicketDeviceEditScreen.kt`, and `InventoryDetailScreen.kt` by adding `modifier = Modifier.imePadding()` (with a `// D5-8:` comment per site explaining the specific inputs it protects) to each `Scaffold(` call. Four of the five files already imported `foundation.layout.*` with a wildcard so the symbol resolved for free; `TicketDeviceEditScreen.kt` used explicit per-symbol imports, so also added `import androidx.compose.foundation.layout.imePadding`. Paired with a manifest fix: `AndroidManifest.xml` `<activity android:name=".MainActivity">` gained `android:windowSoftInputMode="adjustResize"` ‚Äî without it the system sometimes applies `adjustPan` (platform default on some OEM skins), which slides the whole Activity up blindly and defeats `imePadding()`. `adjustResize` is the mode Compose `imePadding` is designed against. Verified with `JAVA_HOME=...Android Studio/jbr ./gradlew.bat :app:compileDebugKotlin` ‚Äî BUILD SUCCESSFUL (pre-existing deprecation warnings only, no new errors). `LoginScreen.kt` already had imePadding on its outer Box, `SmsThreadScreen.kt` / `SmsListScreen.kt` / `CustomerDetailScreen.kt` / every `*CreateScreen.kt` were already covered by prior work. Commit d1c39d9.

Notification offline-path also stamps `isRefreshing = false` on the early-return so a user-initiated pull while offline completes cleanly instead of spinning forever. - [x] D5-6. Walked every `OutlinedTextField` / `TextField` under `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/ui/screens/` that set `imeAction = ImeAction.{Search,Done,Go,Next,Send}` and confirmed which had no matching `KeyboardActions` handler. 51 of 53 ime-action fields across 11 files were bare ‚Äî `LoginScreen.kt` already wired 5 handlers, everything else left the native keyboard's Next/Done/Search/Send glyph inert. Fixes applied per the site's role: (a) **GlobalSearchScreen.kt** ‚Äî added `GlobalSearchViewModel.executeSearch()` that bypasses the 300 ms debounce by `viewModelScope.launch { performSearch(query) }` directly, then wired `keyboardActions = KeyboardActions(onSearch = { focusManager.clearFocus(); viewModel.executeSearch() })` on the inline TopAppBar search field; the reactive-debounced path keeps running for typed input. (b) **BarcodeScanScreen.kt** ‚Äî hoisted the Look Up logic into a local `submit` lambda (`focusManager.clearFocus()` + `onScanned(trimmed)`) and wired both the Search IME key and the on-screen Look Up button through the same closure. (c) form-Create screens (`CustomerCreateScreen.kt`, `LeadCreateScreen.kt`, `ExpenseCreateScreen.kt`, `EmployeeCreateScreen.kt`, `AppointmentCreateScreen.kt`) ‚Äî declared a screen-scoped `focusManager = LocalFocusManager.current` plus reusable `onNext = KeyboardActions(onNext = { focusManager.moveFocus(FocusDirection.Down) })` and, where the last field is ImeAction.Done, `onDoneSave = KeyboardActions(onDone = { focusManager.clearFocus(); viewModel.save() })`. Every field got `keyboardActions = onNext` (or `onDoneSave`) so tapping Next tabs through the form and tapping Done submits. (d) **CustomerDetailScreen.kt** edit panel ‚Äî same Next/Done pattern using `viewModel.saveCustomer()`. Note composer's ImeAction.Send now wires `onSend` to call `onPost()` guarded by `canPost` (draft non-blank + not already posting). (e) **InventoryCreateScreen.kt** / **InventoryEditScreen.kt** share `InventoryFormContent` ‚Äî added an `onSubmit: () -> Unit = {}` parameter on the shared composable, declared `onNext` and `onDoneSubmit` locals inside it so every field routes through the same handlers. Both callers pass `onSubmit = { if (canSave) viewModel.save()/saveItem() }`. (f) **TicketCreateScreen.kt** manual-price field (Step 4 fallback) ‚Äî single Next field, wired directly with a scoped `focusManager` to move focus onto the Continue button. (g) **LoginScreen.kt** ‚Äî filled the two bare Next handlers on the Sign-In username and Set-Password new-password fields, each moving focus forward. Added `FocusDirection` import alongside the already-present `LocalFocusManager`. Counts after the pass: `ImeAction.*` references = `keyboardActions =` references in every file (8/8 CustomerCreate, 10/10 CustomerDetail, 1/1 GlobalSearch, 1/1 BarcodeScan, 7/7 LeadCreate, 1/1 AppointmentCreate, 3/3 ExpenseCreate, 6/6 EmployeeCreate, 8/8 InventoryCreate, 1/1 TicketCreate, 7/7 LoginScreen). - [x] D5-3. Walked `packages/android/app/src/main/java/com/bizarreelectronics/crm/ui/` for every `.clickable(` site. Nine sites chained plain `.clickable(onClick = ...)` on top of a Material3 surface layer (Card, Surface, ListItem, or a Row nested inside BrandCard). With Compose BOM 2025.03 / M3 1.3+, LocalIndication resolution inside those parents silently produced no ripple, so taps felt "ghosted" ‚Äî nothing on screen acknowledged the touch until the network call resolved. Patched three idioms: (a) `Card(...).clickable ‚Üí Card(onClick = ...)` overload for `LeadListScreen.kt` LeadCard, `PosScreen.kt` RecentTicketCard, `SmsTemplatesScreen.kt` SmsTemplateCard; (b) `Surface(...).clickable ‚Üí Surface(onClick = ...)` overload for `SyncStatusBadge.kt` badge root and `LeadDetailScreen.kt` clickable status badge; (c) for Row / ListItem sites that still need `.clickable`, added explicit `interactionSource = remember { MutableInteractionSource() }` + `indication = ripple()` ‚Äî covers `BrandListItem.kt` row, `SmsListScreen.kt` ConversationRow, `CustomerDetailScreen.kt` CustomerTicketHistoryRow, and `AppNavGraph.kt` MoreLogoutRow + MoreRowItem. Ripple import is `androidx.compose.material3.ripple` (M3 moved it out of `material.ripple`). Icon/IconButton sites skipped ‚Äî already ripple via the M3 IconButton composable. Verified with `./gradlew :app:compileDebugKotlin` ‚Äî BUILD SUCCESSFUL. Commit 0b82a03.

- [x] SEC-M47. Migration 105_scheduled_report_recipients.sql creates `scheduled_report_recipients (id, email UNIQUE, enabled, last_sent_at, last_status check(success/failed/skipped), last_error, created_at, updated_at)`. Additive ‚Äî existing single-email tenants keep working via the config-string fallback in `services/scheduledReports.ts`. Follow-up SEC-M47-wire-cron: update the cron to READ from the table first + stamp send status per recipient. Commit 2deffd0.

- [x] SEC-H35. `services/stripe.ts` `handleWebhookEvent` switch adds four cases: `charge.dispute.created` (logs loudly + resolves tenant via `stripe_customer_id` ‚Äî no auto-downgrade since disputes are operator-response events), `charge.refunded` (audit-only log + tenant link so `stripe_webhook_events.tenant_id` is no longer NULL for refund deliveries), `payment_intent.payment_failed` (marks tenant `payment_past_due=1` via customer lookup; does NOT touch `failed_charge_count` because `invoice.payment_failed` is authoritative for dunning and Stripe often fires both), `customer.subscription.trial_will_end` (enqueues an email on the existing `stripe_payment_failure_emails` queue with `attempt_count=0` as the informational-marker; downstream worker can pick subject-line by attempt_count). All four fill `recordedTenantId` so the BL2 idempotency row gets the tenant_id backfilled. Commit da58685.

- [x] SEC-M57. `utils/validate.ts validateRequiredString()` now rejects control codepoints < U+0020 (except TAB/LF/CR) and RTL-override U+202A..U+202E / U+2066..U+2069 via new exported `rejectControlAndRTL()`. Closes log-injection (CR/LF in identifiers splits one log line into two) and presentation-spoofing (RTL flip renders 'TechStore' as 'erotSkceT' in UI lists). Exported helper lets other specific validators opt in. Commit d42dc13.

- [x] SEC-M21. `portal.routes.ts POST /register/send-code` adds a 24h hard cap of 10 codes per phone on top of the existing 3/hour hourly limit. Closes the slow-drip spam vector: 72 codes/day at 20-minute intervals. New rate_limits category `portal_send_code_day`. Over-cap returns 429 'Daily verification cap reached...'. CAPTCHA-on-first-new-IP renamed SEC-M21-captcha + deferred ‚Äî requires CAPTCHA provider integration. Commit 6233747.

- [x] SEC-H38. Migration 104_gift_card_code_hash.sql adds `gift_cards.code_hash` + index; `services/giftCardCodeHashBackfill.ts` hashes legacy rows at boot (idempotent, per-tenant under multi-tenant). `giftCards.routes.ts` lookup now selects on `code_hash`, INSERT writes both plaintext (two-step rollover for existing redemption scripts) + hash, `generateCode` bumped 64‚Üí128 bits (`randomBytes(16)` = 32 hex chars). `audit_log.details` `code` field replaced with `code_prefix` (4 chars) + full `code_hash`. Plaintext code still returned on POST / ONCE for the cashier. Follow-up: drop the plaintext `code` column once all callers are hash-first. Commit 948be32.

- [x] SEC-H51. `POST /estimates/:id/convert` uses a conditional UPDATE as a lock: `UPDATE estimates SET status='converting' WHERE status NOT IN ('converted','cancelled','converting')`. `changes=1` ‚Üí caller wins; `changes=0` ‚Üí 409 "Estimate is already being converted. Try again in a moment." Final UPDATE at :760 flips 'converting' ‚Üí 'converted'. Closes the two-convert race where concurrent clicks could produce two tickets + consume two tier slots from one estimate. Commit 3bb69d8.

- [x] SEC-H50. `POST /estimates/:id/approve` admin-override branch rejects with 403 when `req.user.id === estimate.created_by`. Previously any admin could approve their own estimate, bypassing two-party sign-off. Customer-token branch (where the approval comes from the email/SMS link, not a shop user) unaffected. SELECT grew `created_by` column. Commit f020495.

- [x] SEC-H49. `DELETE /tickets/:id` stock-restore cascade now only credits `ticket_device_parts` rows whose `status` is `'available'` / `'received'` / NULL (legacy). `'missing'` parts never decremented stock to begin with; `'ordered'` parts haven't arrived from the supplier ‚Äî restoring either MINTS inventory. Theft primitive closed: a user who could soft-delete a ticket with missing lines can no longer inflate physical count. Cancel path (F5) already had this invariant; delete now matches. Commit 5d40ec1.

- [x] SEC-H48. `POST /invoices/bulk-action action='void'` now mirrors the stock-restore loop from the single `/:id/void` path (S7 / invoices.routes.ts:674) ‚Äî iterates `invoice_line_items WHERE inventory_item_id IS NOT NULL`, credits `inventory_items.in_stock`, writes `stock_movements` audit rows with `reason='Invoice bulk-voided ‚Äî stock restored'`. Prior bulk branch only flipped status + marked payments voided, permanently decrementing stock on every bulk-voided POS invoice. Either path now lands the shop in the same inventory state. Commit 887f95f.

- [x] SEC-H46. `PUT /repair-pricing/adjustments` tightened `pct` bound from `-100..1000` to `¬±50` (hard reject) with a `confirm_large_adjustment` gate for `20 < |pct| <= 50`. Prior wide bound let a fat-finger / compromised session 11x every repair price in one call. Normal ¬±20% band passes without friction; anything louder requires an explicit confirmation flag the UI can surface as a modal. Commit cf97ef7.

- [x] SEC-H44. `services/stripe.ts` `acquireCustomerLock()` now stamps `stripe_customer_lock_at` (epoch-ms, idempotent `ALTER TABLE tenants ADD COLUMN`) and steals stale locks older than `CUSTOMER_LOCK_TTL_MS = 60_000`. Prior 0/1 flag held forever on mid-acquire crash; every subsequent upgrade attempt 409'd until an operator ran a manual UPDATE. Release nulls both flag + timestamp. Happy path still sub-millisecond; TTL is crash-recovery backstop. Commit 9219854.

- [x] SEC-H37. Migration 103_currency_columns.sql adds `currency TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'USD'` to invoices, payments, refunds, gift_cards, deposits, pos_transactions. Indexed on the 3 tables most likely to get per-currency reports (invoices/payments/refunds). Single-currency tenants keep working ‚Äî existing rows backfill to USD, new INSERTs without an explicit currency still succeed. Paired with SEC-H34-money-refactor (deferred) ‚Äî when REAL‚ÜíINTEGER cents lands, cents + currency will ship together so reports know which minor-unit denomination each row uses. Commit 46bcdf7.

- [x] SEC-H42. `blockchyp.routes.ts POST /process-payment` adds a 30-second dedup against `payment_idempotency WHERE status='completed' AND (invoice_id, amount) matches AND created_at > now()-30s`. Returns 409 with a cashier-readable "wait 30s and retry if intentional" when the window matches ‚Äî BL7 idempotency_key only stopped SAME-key replays, not fresh-key retries from a frustrated cashier after a terminal timeout. IP binding intentionally skipped because CGNAT retries rotate src IP in seconds; invoice_id+amount is the authoritative pair. Commit a04d30b.

- [x] SEC-H43. `blockchyp.routes.ts POST /process-payment` now rejects with 403 when `req.user.role` is not admin/manager. Prior auth-only gate made a compromised cashier session a live-charge primitive (commits shop to settlement fees + refund path regardless of charge outcome). Matches the role gate already on gift-card issuance + refund creation + trade-in accept. Cash/check payments still go through the non-card POS path open to technicians. Commit 72c2b3a.

- [x] SEC-H39. `/pos/transaction` wraps the ticket INSERT in try/catch; on throw `refundTierReservation()` decrements `tenant_usage.tickets_created` by 1 (clamped at 0) so a failed INSERT doesn't permanently burn a free-tier slot. Covers the primary failure window (between reservation commit and first successful row write). Later per-device / invoice INSERTs don't refund because by then the tenant correctly owns a ticket. Best-effort ‚Äî master DB errors during refund don't cascade. Commit e7c4678.

- [x] SEC-H36. `POST /invoices` line-item `tax_amount` now recomputed server-side from `tax_classes.rate` when the line item carries `tax_class_id` ‚Äî matches `pos.routes.ts:413` canonical pattern. Prior code trusted client-supplied `tax_amount` so a hostile POS client could ship 0 and skip state collection. Legacy path (no tax_class_id) still accepts explicit tax_amount to keep pre-tax-class invoices working. Android offline flow intentionally unchanged per TODO note. Commit d489692.

- [x] SA2-1. `tickets.routes.ts` PUT `/:id` customer_id handling hardened: rejects non-number/string types with 400, coerces string ‚Üí int, requires positive integer, writes normalised value back to req.body so the downstream UPDATE binds a primitive. Prior code forwarded object/array shapes directly into better-sqlite3 which surfaced as a 500 with a bind-error stack trace. Commit 633e6b4.

- [x] PROD61. `npm outdated` review: safe patch/minor updates taken (`@tanstack/react-query 5.97‚Üí5.99`, `better-sqlite3 12.8‚Üí12.9`, `stripe 22.0.1‚Üí22.0.2`, `react-router-dom 7.14.0‚Üí7.14.1`). - [x] SEC-H27. `tracking.routes.ts` ‚Äî every public tracking route (`GET /track/:orderId`, `GET /track/portal/:orderId`, `GET /track/portal/:orderId/history`, `POST /track/portal/:orderId/message`, `GET /track/portal/:orderId/invoice`) now reads the tracking token via `extractTrackingToken(req)`, which prefers `Authorization: Bearer <token>` over the legacy `?token=` query parameter. Query-param hits still work during a 90-day deprecation window so old customer email links don't 404, but each one emits a `logger.warn('tracking token supplied via deprecated ?token query parameter', { route, method, user_agent })` so ops can watch client traffic migrate off the query path before the branch is removed (~2026-07-16). `GET /track/token/:token` is unchanged ‚Äî its token sits in the URL path, not the query string, so it does not leak through access-log query patterns. Rationale: bearer-style credentials leaked in query strings end up in web-server access logs, browser history, HTTP Referer headers, and upstream proxy logs; Authorization headers do not. Commit bb51b95.

- [x] SEC-H32. `tracking.routes.ts POST /portal/:orderId/message` ‚Äî added portal-session bypass on top of the existing tracking-token + 3/min IP rate limit. New `extractPortalSessionToken()` + `loadPortalSession()` helpers probe `portal_sessions` using the same credential shape as `portal.routes.ts portalAuth` (Authorization header OR portalToken cookie). If the session is valid AND (scope=full AND ticket.customer_id matches session.customer_id) OR (scope=ticket AND session.ticket_id matches the resolved ticket), the handler skips the tracking-token requirement AND the rate-limit bucket, and records `ticket_history.description = 'Customer left a message via authenticated portal session'` plus a `via: 'portal_session'` marker in the response. Anonymous/tracking-token callers keep the exact pre-fix behavior: 3 messages per minute per IP, tracking_token required, generic history description. Also touches `portal_sessions.last_used_at` when the session is used so portal idle-timeout (4h) stays in sync. Net: full-portal customers can reply without hitting the anti-abuse cap, bad actors are still throttled. Commit 63620f6.

- [x] SEC-M20. `management.routes.ts` ‚Äî documented the per-handler tenantId validation invariant at the top of the file. All three mutating tenant endpoints (`POST /tenants/:slug/suspend`, `/activate`, `DELETE /tenants/:slug`) already: (a) accept the tenant id ONLY via URL path param `:slug`, (b) run `validateSlugParam` (rejects anything outside `^[a-z0-9]([a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?$`, max 30 chars), (c) `SELECT id, status FROM tenants WHERE slug = ?` in master DB and 404 if not found, (d) route through canonical helpers in `services/tenant-provisioning.ts` (suspendTenant/activateTenant/deleteTenant) so pool close + plan cache bust + WebSocket disconnect + soft-delete grace all happen in one place, and (e) write `managementAudit()` rows with `tenant_id`, `previous_status`, and operator IP. No handler accepts a `tenantId` or `tenantSlug` from body/query. Super-admin JWT is enforced upstream by `managementAuth` (role + `super_admins.is_active = 1`). No code change ‚Äî the invariant is codified in a docstring so future mutating endpoints follow the recipe. Commit 51afe9f.

- [x] DEBUG-SEC1. Bare-IP dev tenantResolver bypass hardened with a two-key gate: `NODE_ENV !== 'production'` AND `APP_ENV === 'development'`. Production sets only NODE_ENV; an operator would have to affirmatively set APP_ENV=development to re-enable the bypass ‚Äî matches DEBUG-SEC1(b) intent. - [x] PROD52. Correlation ID middleware in `index.ts` (mounted right after the HTTPS redirect, before helmet/cors) attaches `res.locals.requestId` and echoes `X-Request-Id` on every response. - [x] SEC-H20-partial. Super-admin JWT `expiresIn` shortened from `4h` to `30m` (`super-admin.routes.ts:19`). - [x] SEC-M17. `tradeIns.routes.ts` PATCH `/:id` ‚Äî accepting a trade-in now commits an inventory row and store credit atomically with the status flip. Previously the handler only updated `trade_ins` and left inventory + store credit to separate follow-up calls that could silently never run (or run twice, or run after a crash). New flow: pull existing `status, customer_id, device_name, condition, accepted_price` up front; detect the "was-not-accepted ‚Üí is-now-accepted AND effective accepted_price > 0" transition, build a `TxQuery[]` batch containing (a) the UPDATE on trade_ins, (b) an INSERT into inventory_items (name=device_name, item_type='product', device_type='trade_in:<condition>', cost/retail=accepted_price, in_stock=1, is_active=1), (c) store_credits balance upsert (read-then-branch because 026_refunds_credits.sql has no UNIQUE(customer_id) ‚Äî falls back to UPDATE if the row exists, INSERT if not), (d) store_credit_transactions ledger row (`type='manual_credit'`, `reference_type='trade_in'`, `reference_id=trade_in_id`, `notes='Trade-in credit'`). Inventory INSERT always runs on accept (simplest path); store credit only mints when customer_id is set (null customer_id is a valid state for walk-in / one-off trade-ins, ledger stays clean). Audit entry grows `accepted_transition` + `store_credit_issued` fields. Commit bdab160.

- [x] SEC-L18. `index.ts` ‚Äî new per-tenant failure circuit wraps the tenant-retention-sweep (hourly‚Üídaily at 02:00 local) and appointment-reminder (every 15 min) cron handlers. One bad tenant (corrupt DB, schema drift, wedged SMS provider) used to burn CPU on every subsequent tick forever ‚Äî the inner try/catch swallowed errors but the same doomed code path re-ran every tick. Added `cronCircuits: Map<string, {consecutiveFailures, openUntil}>` alongside the existing `cronLastRun` map, with helpers `circuitAllowsRun`, `recordCircuitFailure`, `recordCircuitSuccess` keyed on `(cronName, tenantSlug ?? 'default')`. After 5 consecutive failures the tenant is skipped for 10 minutes before retrying; any success clears the counter and the open window both. For appointment reminders, a per-message SMS failure does NOT count as a tenant-level failure (bad phone numbers and transient provider errors are bounded by design); only an uncaught tenant-work failure rolls up. Circuit state is in-memory per-process ‚Äî cron jobs only run on one node so this is fine. Commit 4414d5c.

- [x] SEC-M43. `pos.routes.ts` `/checkout-with-ticket` ‚Äî card-method overpayment now routes excess to store credit instead of silently dropping it. Previously `change = max(0, paid - total)` fired on every payment method, including card. On cash that's correct (hand back a bill); on card BlockChyp had charged the full amount but the invoice clamped amount_paid to total and the rest evaporated. New flow: card tenders (`card`, `credit`, `debit`, `blockchyp`, `stripe`) get their overpayment captured into `cardOverpayment`; in split-payment mode, cash tenders first cover the invoice total and only the card-method excess is store-credited (prevents mixed $50 cash + $100 card on a $90 invoice from losing the card excess). All payment inserts + POS transaction insert + store_credits upsert + store_credit_transactions ledger INSERT now build a `TxQuery[]` batch and run under one `adb.transaction()`. store_credits upsert uses the same read-then-branch pattern as SEC-M17. Ledger fields: `type='manual_credit'`, `reference_type='card_overpayment'`, `reference_id=invoice_id`, notes identifying the method. Response now exposes `store_credit_issued` so the UI can show the split instead of silently pocketing. Commit 1c0f73a.

- [x] SEC-M44. New migration `100_payment_capture_state.sql` adds a `capture_state TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'captured' CHECK (capture_state IN ('authorized','captured','voided'))` column to `payments` plus an index on that column. Backfills defensively (`UPDATE payments SET capture_state = 'captured' WHERE capture_state IS NULL`). `refunds.routes.ts` POST `/` now rejects with 400 when any payment on the target invoice has `capture_state != 'captured'` ‚Äî blocks refunding money that was never captured (auth-only) or already released (voided). Error message names the count and the distinct non-captured states so the operator knows whether to capture or void first. Uses `COALESCE(capture_state, 'captured')` for defense-in-depth against any row that somehow escapes the backfill. `blockchyp.routes.ts` charge INSERT now writes `capture_state='captured'` explicitly since BlockChyp charges capture immediately on approval; making it explicit removes the silent dependency on the column default. Stripe INSERT sites: none currently exist server-side (Stripe flows today go through webhook paths that don't insert into payments); default 'captured' covers any future direct INSERTs. Commit 1fe0f60.

- [x] SEC-M51. `auth.routes.ts` TOTP encryption key derivation ‚Äî v3 replaces raw `SHA-256(jwt+sa)` with HKDF-based (RFC 5869) derivation using `crypto.hkdfSync('sha256', Buffer.from(jwt+sa), Buffer.from('bizarre-totp-salt-v3'), Buffer.from('totp-key-v3'), 32)` and binds the version tag as AES-GCM AAD via `cipher.setAAD(Buffer.from('v3'))`. HKDF's extract/expand pattern gives a proper PRF with salt injection and `info`/IKM/salt domain separation; raw SHA-256 over a concatenated string provides none of that. AAD binding closes a theoretical downgrade-by-prefix-rewrite: tampering the version prefix on `v3:iv:tag:data` now fails the GCM auth tag (verified manually ‚Äî rewriting v3‚Üív4 fails with `Unsupported state or unable to authenticate data`). v1/v2 legacy keys stay in `ENCRYPTION_KEYS` for decrypt; `decryptSecret` only calls `setAAD` when `version >= 3` so all pre-existing ciphertexts continue to read unchanged. New encrypts route through `CURRENT_KEY_VERSION=3`. `super-admin.routes.ts:94,103` is still using the old `sha256(sa + ':totp:superadmin')` pattern ‚Äî separate follow-up; out of scope for this commit. Commit e85a2e1.

- [x] SEC-H18. `middleware/auth.ts:185` `requirePermission()` evaluation order flipped: customRolePermissions now runs BEFORE the `users.role === 'admin'` bypass. Previously an admin assigned a narrow custom role via `PUT /roles/users/:userId/role` (which writes `user_custom_roles` only, not `users.role`) kept full permissions because the admin bypass short-circuited. Now the custom role is authoritative when assigned; legacy admin bypass still applies when no custom role is pinned (prevents org lockout). Commit 2a99b6b.

- [x] CROSS38b-notif. Android Settings > Notifications preferences sub-page. New `NotificationSettingsScreen.kt` (VM + Composable) wired via a new `Screen.NotificationSettings` route (`settings/notifications`). Six toggle rows split across two cards: Delivery channels (Email alerts / SMS alerts / Push notifications) and Categories (Low-stock / New-ticket / Appointment-reminder). Each backed by a new boolean on `AppPreferences` (`notifEmailAlertsEnabled`, `notifSmsAlertsEnabled`, `notifPushEnabled`, `notifLowStockEnabled`, `notifNewTicketEnabled`, `notifAppointmentReminderEnabled`) defaulting ON. `SettingsScreen` gains a new `onNotificationSettings: (() -> Unit)?` callback and renders a top-level "Notifications" `SettingsRow` using the same card-with-clickable-row shape as Edit Profile, sitting under SETTINGS. `AppNavGraph` registers the route, the SettingsScreen composable passes `onNotificationSettings = { navController.navigate(Screen.NotificationSettings.route) }`, and the NotificationSettings composable pops back on its own back button. Distinct from the notifications INBOX (`NotificationListScreen`) per CROSS54 ‚Äî this configures which events fire; the inbox lists events that already fired.

- [x] PROD12. Migration 101_pin_set_flag.sql adds `users.pin_set INTEGER DEFAULT 0`. `/auth/switch-user` rejects with 403 + `code: 'PIN_NOT_SET'` when matched user's pin_set is 0 (still on provisioning default '1234'). `/auth/change-pin` flips pin_set ‚Üí 1 on success. Mirrors password_set flow. Existing users forced to rotate on next switch ‚Äî safer default than silently accepting 1234. Commit fceebbe.

- [x] PROD32. `index.ts` ‚Äî HSTS header now only emitted in production via a `hstsConfig` constant (`config.nodeEnv === 'production' ? { maxAge: 15552000, includeSubDomains: true } : false`). Prior config sent `max-age=63072000; includeSubDomains; preload` unconditionally, which burned the self-signed dev cert into every local browser cache and required a manual `chrome://net-internals/#hsts` purge on a fresh checkout. 180-day max-age matches the TODO.md spec and gives operators a reasonable rotation window without locking clients out on a cert swap. `preload` intentionally omitted ‚Äî hstspreload.org registration is a separate opt-in decision once the operator controls a real apex cert. Commit c145c7f.

- [x] PROD33. Audit of all 5 `res.cookie()` call sites in `packages/server/src`: `auth.routes.ts:271` (refreshToken on login), `:828` (deviceTrust), `:1024` (refresh rotation), `:1179` (impersonation), and `utils/csrf.ts:32` (portalCsrfToken). All had `HttpOnly` (except CSRF intentionally JS-readable for the double-submit pattern) and `SameSite` already set ‚Äî but `Secure` was hardcoded `true`, which silently drops the cookie on any dev tooling that talks plain HTTP. Gated `Secure` on `config.nodeEnv === 'production'` on all five so prod still forces HTTPS-only cookies while dev over HTTP (test tablets / curl) gets a usable session. No change to HttpOnly/SameSite/path/maxAge semantics. Auth cookies keep `SameSite=strict`; CSRF keeps `SameSite=lax` + `httpOnly=false` per double-submit design. Commit f706cbf.

- [x] PROD34. `index.ts` helmet CSP audit ‚Äî docs-only outcome, already tight. Global CSP: `default-src 'self'`, `script-src 'self' https://static.cloudflareinsights.com` (NO `'unsafe-inline'` in global CSP for prod OR dev ‚Äî Vite HMR uses `<script src=>` + eventsource, not inline), `script-src-attr 'self'` (no inline onclick handlers), `frame-ancestors 'none'` globally with per-tenant allowlist on `/widget`. `style-src 'unsafe-inline'` retained intentionally ‚Äî Tailwind runtime utilities and React-injected `<style>` tags require it; style-injection blast radius is far smaller than script injection. Documented exceptions: `/admin` and `/super-admin` HTML routes set a relaxed per-route CSP with script `'unsafe-inline'` for legacy inline onclick handlers in the backup panel ‚Äî both routes are localhost-only, scoped override not a global relaxation. Added PROD34 block comment above global `helmet()` call and expanded comment on `adminCsp` constant so a future auditor doesn't re-derive what's tight vs. relaxed. Commit c3738a7.

- [x] PROD36. `index.ts:799-856` CORS config audit + harden. Prior inline origin callback mixed the no-origin fast path with the allowlist match, making it easy for a future refactor to accidentally short-circuit and reflect an unvetted origin while `credentials: true` is set (the classic CORS-spec violation). Extracted the match into `isCorsOriginAllowed(origin)` so the rule is: no Origin -> `callback(null, true)` (no ACAO emitted anyway, credentials moot); origin in allowedOrigins / BASE_DOMAIN + subdomains / LAN (dev only) -> reflect; anything else -> reject with `new Error('CORS not allowed')`. Added PROD36 comment block making explicit that credentials can only ride on a reflected explicit origin, never on `*`. No behavior change for legitimate clients; hardens against future refactor drift. Commit b2ca864.

- [x] PROD37. `ws/server.ts` WebSocket upgrade audit. Existing protections verified: `index.ts:670-685` `verifyClient` rejects bad Origin with 403 BEFORE socket accept (SEC-WS1, mirrors HTTP CORS allowlist); 5-second `authTimeoutHandle` terminates any socket that has not sent a valid `{type:'auth', token}` frame; invalid JWT closes with 1008 + clears timer; per-socket 60/min rate limit closes with 1008. Gap closed: an unauthenticated socket that sent a non-auth message used to log a warning, reply with an `error` frame, and leave the socket open for the full 5s window ‚Äî a scanner could hold sockets open and burn fd + heap. Now `close(1008, 'not authenticated')` fires on the first non-auth inbound, shrinking the window from 5s to one message round-trip. Token-at-handshake (query param / subprotocol) kept out of scope ‚Äî browser WebSocket constructor cannot set custom headers, and moving the check earlier would require concurrent web + Android client rewrites. Commit bb191b9.

- [x] CROSS9a. Ticket history section on Android `CustomerDetailScreen`. Added `CustomerApi.getTickets(id, page=1, pageSize=10)` hitting the existing server endpoint `GET /customers/:id/tickets` which returns `{ tickets: [TicketListItem], pagination }` ‚Äî same shape as the main ticket list so `TicketListData` is reused without a new DTO. `CustomerDetailViewModel` fires a third parallel fetch (`ticketsJob`) alongside detail + analytics; null state = still loading or silent-degrade after fetch failure, empty list = loaded with no tickets. `CustomerDetailContent` picks up a new `recentTickets: List<TicketListItem>?` parameter and renders a `BrandCard` "Ticket history" section between the quick-stats row and the Call/SMS action row (matches the spec wording "under the quick-stats row"). Each row is `T-XXXXX (mono) ¬∑ device name ¬∑ BrandStatusBadge ¬∑ $price`, tap routes to `TicketDetail` via the existing `onNavigateToTicket` callback. Max 10 rows enforced client-side via `.take(10)`. CROSS9 parent split into CROSS9a (done), CROSS9b-needs-api (notes ‚Äî no server endpoint), CROSS9c (addresses), CROSS9d (tag chips).

- [x] SEC-H19. `startAutoClockoutSweep` in `employees.routes.ts:618` now iterates every active tenant DB in multi-tenant mode instead of running once against `config.dbPath` (which points at master in MT). Branches: MT ‚Üí SELECT slugs from master + `getTenantDb(slug)` + `createAsyncDb(pooled.name)` per tenant; single-tenant preserved. Per-tenant errors log + skip so one broken DB doesn't block the rest. Before: every tenant's stale clock entries stayed open forever. Commit 70c0325.

- [x] SEC-H17. Migration 100_recovery_cooldown.sql adds `users.last_backup_recovery_at`. `/auth/recover-with-backup-code` stamps the column on success. `PUT /settings/users/:id` now rejects role changes with 403 for 24h after the target's last recovery (`Role cannot be changed for Nh after a backup-code recovery`). Closes the vector where an attacker with a stolen backup code + leaked email could run recovery and immediately escalate / demote other admins before the real user notices. Password/PIN change within the window still allowed. Commit 8d90bfc.

- [x] NEW-TLIST-GRP. Android ticket list rows now render a small group pill to the LEFT of the specific status badge so the high-level bucket is scannable at a glance. Added private `TicketStatusGroup` enum + `ticketStatusGroupFor(TicketEntity)` mapper to `TicketListScreen.kt` with inference rules: `statusIsClosed && !looksCancelled ‚Üí Complete (green)`, `name contains cancel/void ‚Üí Cancelled (grey)`, `name contains waiting ‚Üí Waiting (tertiary/amber)`, else `In Progress (primary/orange)`. Rendered as a compact `Surface` pill (`surfaceVariant` bg + single-hue label text) matching the `BrandStatusBadge` visual weight, with a 6dp spacer between the group pill and the specific status badge. Non-breaking for the existing trailing-column layout (pill + badge live in a nested `Row`, the money line stays on the second line). Because `TicketEntity` does not carry a dedicated `is_cancelled` column (only `statusIsClosed`), cancellation is inferred from the status-name heuristic ‚Äî same style the spec already allowed for the Waiting group.

- [x] SEC-H33. Payment-link public routes verified as DB-level tenant-isolated: `payment_links` has no `tenant_id` column because the architecture uses a per-tenant SQLite file. Global `tenantResolver` middleware (`index.ts:967`) rewrites `req.asyncDb` to the per-tenant DB based on Host subdomain, so a token minted in tenant A's file cannot be found via tenant B's Host. Added code comment documenting the invariant so future reviewers don't re-flag. Commit 6fa69dc.

- [x] NEW-MSG-EMPTYHINT. Android Messages empty-state subtext updated from "Tap the edit icon to start a new conversation" to "Tap the + button to start a new conversation" at `SmsListScreen.kt:262`. Post-CROSS42 the new-conversation action is a FAB (pencil/plus) at bottom-right, so the prior wording pointed users at a non-existent edit icon in the top bar.

- [x] SEC-H24. `tracking.routes.ts:77` `toPublicTicket()` no longer includes `tracking_token` in the unauth `/track/:orderId` response. Token is a 32-char random bearer credential ‚Äî returning it in a public lookup let any probe with a valid order_id harvest the token and reuse it on other portal paths to impersonate the customer. Authenticated `/customers/:id/tickets` still returns it (role-gated). SMS-OTP-gated reveal remains future work. Commit e4fc965.

- [x] SEC-M60. `paymentLinks.routes.ts` ‚Äî `/:token/click` and `/:token/pay` now reject with 410 Gone when `expires_at` is in the past. Prior code only enforced `status = 'active'` which left active-but-stale rows replayable until someone hit GET (which is the only handler that auto-flipped `status` to `'expired'`). Both mutation endpoints now SELECT `expires_at` alongside the row, flip to `'expired'` when the check fires, and throw `new AppError('Payment link has expired', 410)`. Portal UI can read 410 as "permanently unavailable ‚Äî ask shop for a new link" instead of treating it like a transient failure.

- [x] SEC-M45. Portal `portalAuth` middleware now enforces a 4-hour idle timeout on top of the existing 24-hour absolute `expires_at`. Pulls `last_used_at` on lookup; if stale, DELETEs the session row and returns 401 `Session idle timeout. Please log in again.` Active users (who touch `last_used_at` every request) never kicked. Closes the shared-workstation resume-as-previous-customer vector. CSRF synchronizer-token migration out of scope this pass ‚Äî separate work. Commit c1f8dc9.

- [x] SEC-M59. `estimates.routes.ts:893-926` ‚Äî NULL `approval_token_expires_at` no longer means "never expires". Previously the expiry branch was gated on truthy check which silently skipped enforcement for legacy rows signed before the expiry-policy migration, leaving leaked pre-policy links replayable indefinitely. Now the code explicitly rejects with 410 Gone (`"Estimate approval token has no expiry ‚Äî signed before expiry policy rolled out; ask shop to reissue"`) so the shop has to reissue the estimate. The 410 status (vs 403) tells email clients / portal UI the resource is permanently unavailable so UX can render a clear "ask for a fresh link" message instead of looking like a generic auth failure.

- [x] SEC-M50. `db/tenant-pool.ts:104` ‚Äî no code change. `busy_timeout = 5000` was already correct. Added a rationale comment documenting the choice: multiple crons (session cleanup, payment-idempotency janitor, retention sweeps, appointment reminder) race on the same tenant DB when tick intervals overlap, and the 5s window serializes writers instead of letting SQLite return `SQLITE_BUSY` immediately. 5s covers normal DELETE / WAL checkpoint + safety, short enough that a genuinely stuck writer is surfaced rather than papered over for minutes. Raising this would mask real deadlocks; lowering causes flaky retention runs on busy tenants.

- [x] SEC-M54. `/estimates/bulk-convert` now refunds unused quota slots via `UPDATE tenant_usage SET tickets_created = MAX(0, tickets_created - failCount)` after the conversion loop. Prior flow atomically reserved `estimateCount` up-front and kept every slot even if mid-loop failures (not-found / already-converted) left fewer real tickets created ‚Äî permanent over-charge against monthly plan limit. Best-effort refund: master DB failures log without throwing, so the user's mixed-result response isn't replaced by a 500. Runs only on multi-tenant + finite tier. Commit b9c0db7.

- [x] SEC-M49. `index.ts` ‚Äî new daily per-tenant DB size observability cron. Fires once per UTC day during hour 02 (between the 02:00 tenant-timezone retention sweeps and the 03:00 master retention sweep), guarded by `shouldRunDaily('tenant-db-size-monitor', 'UTC')` so it runs exactly once even if the hourly interval lands multiple times in the window. Per tenant, it reads `tenantDb.name` (the better-sqlite3 file path), calls `fs.statSync(dbFile).size`, and emits one `log.info('tenant db size', { slug, sizeBytes, sizeMB })`. No archival, no delete ‚Äî that belongs to SEC-AL5 (audit logs) and the retention sweeper respectively. One syscall per tenant per day, negligible budget. Ops can chart DB growth over time and catch a runaway tenant before it stalls the whole node on a full disk.

- [x] SEC-M46. New `deleteStripeCustomer(id)` helper exported from `services/stripe.ts` (returns false if Stripe not configured, idempotent on 404). `archiveDueTenants()` in `services/tenant-provisioning.ts:615` promoted to async and now best-effort-deletes the Stripe customer when `tenants.stripe_customer_id` is set before flipping status to 'deleted'. Failures log warn and archive proceeds ‚Äî dead tenant shouldn't hang on Stripe 5xx. Closes PII-retention gap on archive. Commit fa72b3c.

- [x] CROSS50-header-needs-api. Quick-stats row under the customer avatar now renders ticket count, lifetime value, and last-visit relative time. `CustomerDto.kt` gains a `CustomerAnalytics` data class matching the server's `{ total_tickets, lifetime_value, avg_ticket_value, first_visit, last_visit, days_since_last_visit }` payload; `CustomerApi.getAnalytics(id)` hits `GET /customers/:id/analytics`. `CustomerDetailViewModel` constructor-injects `CustomerApi` and fires `loadAnalytics()` in parallel with `loadCustomer()` ‚Äî a separate `analyticsJob` cancel/relaunch so `loadCustomer()` can retry independently. UiState gains a nullable `analytics: CustomerAnalytics?`; a failed fetch leaves it null and the row silently doesn't render. `CustomerDetailContent` picks up a new `analytics` parameter and (when non-null) renders a three-column `Row(Arrangement.SpaceEvenly)` with `QuickStat` children: Tickets (count), Lifetime ($N whole dollars), Last visit (`DateFormatter.formatRelative` on the ISO string). Analytics row sits between the avatar and the Call/SMS button row so the detail starts with STATE then ACTION. No DTO schema migration needed on the Android side ‚Äî the analytics response is a parallel fetch, not an addition to `CustomerDetail`. Commit 5c280e9.

- [x] CROSS47-wizard-avatar. Ticket wizard customer-search results now render the shared `CustomerAvatar` initial-circle composable (`ui/components/shared/CustomerAvatar.kt`) as their leading content instead of the generic `Icons.Default.Person` glyph ‚Äî same visual treatment as `CustomerListRow` and `GlobalSearchScreen` customer hits. `TicketCreateScreen.kt` picker list's `ListItem.leadingContent` swaps out the `Icon(Person)` for `CustomerAvatar(name = buildCustomerName(customer))`. Pure render change; no state / wiring / DTO changes. Commit bef06d4.

- [x] CROSS56. Customer Edit Tags placeholder already switched from developer-placeholder `"tag1, tag2, tag3"` to tenant-relevant `"VIP, corporate, loyalty"` (`CustomerDetailScreen.kt:460`). Introduced by commit 3b86f9b. The autocomplete-from-existing-tenant-tags follow-on is still future work but the immediate "looks like leftover placeholder" UX bug is closed.

- [x] SEC-M56. `sms.routes.ts` ‚Äî two-part hardening. (1) Per-destination rate limit: before inserting the outbound row we call `consumeWindowRate(req.db, 'sms_per_destination', convPhone, 3, 3600_000)` so at most 3 messages/hour can be sent to the same normalized phone number. Keyed on `convPhone` so "+15551234567" and "(555) 123-4567" hit the same counter. Prevents buggy integrations / template-render loops from hammering one customer with dozens of messages in a few minutes. (2) Phone redaction in logs: new `redactPhone()` helper masks the carrier prefix and keeps only last 4 (`XXX-XXX-4567`). Applied to `logger.warn('outbound sms not delivered', { to, ... })` -> `{ toRedacted, ... }` and `logger.info('sms auto-reply sent off-hours', { from })` -> `{ fromRedacted }`. Customer phone numbers no longer land unredacted in the ops log aggregator / shared dashboard.

- [x] SEC-M58. `services/dunningScheduler.ts:408` `cutoffDateIso()` now takes a `timeZone` param; callsite reads `store_config.store_timezone` via new `getTenantTimezone()` helper. Uses `Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', { timeZone })` for clean YYYY-MM-DD in tenant zone. Prior UTC cutoff produced 7h early/late drift on non-UTC tenants around DST, causing embarrassing 11 PM SMS sends. No new deps. Commit 6e9268c.

- [x] SEC-M55. `sms.routes.ts:414-440` ‚Äî POST `/sms/send` now enforces a per-tenant daily outbound cap in addition to the existing 5/min per-user window limiter. Before inserting the outbound row we run `SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sms_messages WHERE direction='outbound' AND status NOT IN ('failed','simulated') AND created_at > datetime('now','-1 day')` and throw a 429 once the count hits `DAILY_TENANT_SMS_CAP` (default 500, override via env `TENANT_SMS_DAILY_CAP`). `'sending'` and `'scheduled'` rows are included in the count so in-flight messages debit the ceiling and a burst cannot race past the limit before statuses settle. Carrier-fraud containment: bounds a compromised tenant / stolen API token to at most 500 messages/day instead of 7200 (what the 5/min limiter allows at steady drip).

- [x] SEC-M41. Migration 099 adds `user_id` column to `payment_idempotency` + new `UNIQUE(invoice_id, client_request_id, user_id)`. `blockchyp.routes.ts:178` lookup + reserve INSERT now include `req.user!.id`. Prior narrow UNIQUE let a stolen `(invoice_id, idempotency_key)` pair replay from another user's session and leak original charge's transaction_id/amount via the 'replayed' happy path. Existing rows backfilled from `invoices.created_by`. Commit 8e727cd.

- [x] SEC-M52. `index.ts:792-817` production CORS no longer auto-accepts RFC1918 / CGNAT / localhost origins. The LAN / loopback regex now runs only when `config.nodeEnv !== 'production'` so prod is narrowed to `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` + `BASE_DOMAIN` (+ subdomains). Dev retains the permissive rule so shop tablets can hit the server by LAN IP during testing. If an operator wants to whitelist a LAN origin in prod they must add it explicitly to `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` in the env. Closes the browser-extension / shared-host spoof path where a malicious neighbor on the LAN forges an `Origin: http://192.168.x.x` to bypass CORS against the public API.

- [x] SEC-M37. `inventory.routes.ts:1680` quick-add now runs `cost_price` / `retail_price` through `validatePrice()` (400 on non-finite / negative); empty/undefined still defaults to 0 for the convenience flow. `repairPricing.routes.ts:45-46` gains a local `safeNum()` wrapping `parseFloat` + `Number.isFinite` check when reading `repair_price_flat_adjustment` / `repair_price_pct_adjustment` from `store_config` so bad rows can't turn into Infinity in downstream arithmetic. Commit ad7cc2e.

- [x] CROSS47-seed. Android ticket wizard now accepts and pre-seeds customerId from a nav arg. `Screen.TicketCreate` gained a `createRoute(customerId: Long? = null)` builder and the composable is registered with an optional `customerId` query arg. `TicketCreateViewModel` injects `SavedStateHandle`, reads the arg on init, and a new `setPickedCustomer(id)` helper resolves the row via `CustomerRepository.getCustomer(id).filterNotNull().firstOrNull()` then populates `UiState.selectedCustomer` and advances to the Category step ‚Äî same end-state as tapping a search result. Idempotent: if the user already picked a customer (or walk-in) between launch and the flow completing, the seeder no-ops. Bottom-nav visibility check updated from `== Screen.TicketCreate.route` to `.startsWith(...)` since the registered route template now carries the `?customerId={customerId}` suffix. CustomerDetail's onCreateTicket callback now calls `createRoute(customerId)`. Commit d46d70e.

- [x] CROSS22-badge-cap. - [x] SEC-M62. `DELETE /tickets/:id` now gated on `requirePermission('tickets.delete')` and hard-blocks when the associated invoice has any `amount_paid > 0`. Prior route was auth-only so any logged-in user could cascade-delete tickets, triggering stock restores and invoice voids. Paid-invoice delete is now rejected regardless of the allow-delete-after-invoice toggle ‚Äî the admin must refund first so the revenue event is debited, not erased. Commit a56e7bb.

- [x] SEC-L39. Recurring appointment auto-generation (`leads.routes.ts:477`) now uses `addMonthsClamped()` that pivots to day-1 before `setMonth` and clamps to the target month's last valid day. Prior `setMonth(getMonth()+i)` silently rolled Jan 31 ‚Üí Mar 3 on non-leap years (and April 31 ‚Üí May 1). Weekly/biweekly unchanged ‚Äî `setDate()` already exact across DST for the server's TZ. date-fns not pulled in (would be a new dep) ‚Äî native Date is sufficient for this clamp. Commit 6ede85a.

- [x] SEC-L23. `services/stripe.ts` exports `resetStripeClient()` that sets the module-level `stripeClient` back to null. Any super-admin path that rotates STRIPE_SECRET_KEY at runtime can now call this helper; the next `getStripe()` lazy-inits a fresh client with the new key. Previously the singleton was cached for process lifetime so a rotated key was silently ignored until restart. Commit 761a1ae.

- [x] SEC-L27. Portal `widget.js` now validates `data-server` against a CNAME pattern `https://<sub>.<domain>.<tld>[:port][/path]` (dev exemption for localhost / 127.0.0.1). Prior code accepted any string, so a malicious embedder could point the widget at an attacker-controlled origin and render a lookalike portal to phish customer credentials. Commit a89ff84.

- [x] SEC-L44. 2FA backup codes switched from 32-char hex to 16-char Crockford base32 formatted `XXXX-XXXX-XXXX-XXXX` in `auth.routes.ts:780`. Crockford alphabet (0-9 A-Z minus I L O U) excludes confusable pairs so users typing codes off paper don't fat-finger 0/O or 1/l/I. 80 bits of entropy ‚Äî still well above NIST's 10^-6 guess-rate bar for 8 single-use codes. Verify path unchanged (bcrypt.compareSync is format-agnostic); already-enrolled users keep working. Absorbed into commit d46d70e via concurrent-session git interleave (wrong commit message ‚Äî real content change is the Crockford swap in `auth.routes.ts:776-800`).

- [x] SEC-L40. `invoices.routes.ts` payment_plan validator now cross-checks `installments * amount_per ‚âà invoice.total` with tolerance `$0.01 + installments * $0.01` for penny-split rounding. Prior checks validated each field in isolation so 6 √ó $10 on a $100 invoice could be saved. Mismatch rejects with 400 and a message showing both sums. Commit fb325aa.

- [x] SEC-L38. Boot-time `import_runs` zombie recovery added to `index.ts` (runs alongside the SMS sweep after `migrateAllTenants()`). Per-tenant UPDATE marks any `import_runs.status IN ('running', 'pending')` as `failed` with `error_log` entry tagged `zombie-recovery: import crashed / server restarted before completion`. Also DELETEs stale `import_locks` rows so new imports can start. Commit b6562fa.

- [x] SEC-L42. `/signup` validation errors ‚Äî malformed email, invalid-format slug, slug-already-taken ‚Äî now all return one generic `Signup failed. Please check your details and try again.` instead of three distinct strings. Prior differences let probes enumerate taken slugs (AZ-042). Validation still runs; specific reason flows to `logger.warn` for operator debugging, never to the wire. Per-email rate limit 429 message unchanged. Commit cf6e581.

- [x] SEC-L29. `paymentLinks.routes.ts` public-route token validators (GET /:token, POST /:token/click, POST /:token/pay) now check `^[A-Za-z0-9_-]{32}$` ‚Äî matching the 24-byte/32-char base64url output of `generateToken()` exactly. Prior `length >= 8` guard let 62^8-space garbage reach the DB lookup. Commit 1d0a0cb.

- [x] CROSS45-ext. `BrandWaveDivider` (`ui/components/WaveDivider.kt`) was pulling its hairline color from `MaterialTheme.colorScheme.tertiary`. - [x] CROSS15. `TicketCreateScreen.kt` step 2 label renamed from "Category" to "Device Type". - [x] CROSS10. Walk-in ghost button landed on the Android ticket wizard customer step, parity with web CROSS4. - [x] CROSS32-ext. Extended CROSS32's money-input affordance (`leadingIcon = { Text("$") }` + `placeholder = "0.00"`) to the last three holdouts that were still using the old `prefix = { Text("$") }` slot with no placeholder: `invoices/InvoiceDetailScreen.kt:261` payment Amount, `expenses/ExpenseCreateScreen.kt:219` Amount, `pos/CheckoutScreen.kt:450` Cash amount. - [x] SEC-L33. HTTPS `tlsOptions` now pins a modern AEAD cipher whitelist (`TLS_AES_256_GCM_SHA384`, `TLS_CHACHA20_POLY1305_SHA256`, `TLS_AES_128_GCM_SHA256`, `ECDHE-ECDSA-AES256-GCM-SHA384`, `ECDHE-RSA-AES256-GCM-SHA384`, ECDHE-*-CHACHA20-POLY1305, ECDHE-*-AES128-GCM-SHA256) and sets `honorCipherOrder: true`. Prior reliance on Node defaults meant a downgrade-happy client could negotiate CBC-mode suites. Commit 9b09a9a.

- [x] SEC-L37. `/sms/send` in `sms.routes.ts:425` now rejects `to` values that don't normalise to 8-15 digits with `Recipient phone is not a valid E.164 number`. Prior code only length-checked `to` (‚â§30 chars), so "hello", "", emoji, and short digit strings dropped straight through to the provider ‚Äî billable reject + audit noise, and some providers silently swallow malformed destinations into false "delivered" callbacks. Commit 4a3ca61.

- [x] SEC-L35. Boot-time zombie recovery added to `index.ts` (runs once after `migrateAllTenants()`). Per-tenant UPDATE marks any `sms_messages.status = 'sending'` older than 10 minutes as `failed` with tag `zombie-recovery: stuck in sending > 10m after server restart`. Previously stranded rows stayed in 'sending' forever after a crash mid-dispatch, blocking retry UI. Commit 2963767.

- [x] SEC-L36. `sms.routes.ts:543` now awaits `incrementSmsCount(req.tenantId)` inside a try/catch and tags the sms_messages row with `;usage_untracked` on failure. Prior fire-and-forget `.then().catch()` silently skipped the counter on any crash path, letting attackers bypass plan quota via any route that reliably crashed the tracker. Fail-closed here means observable (ops can WHERE-clause the tag) ‚Äî the provider already accepted the send so we can't un-send. Commit 628674d.

- [x] SEC-L31. Outbound webhook HMAC now signs `${timestamp}.${body}` instead of body-only (`services/webhooks.ts:257`). Prior scheme shipped X-Webhook-Timestamp unauthenticated, so a replay attacker could swap the header and fool a freshness-checking receiver into re-accepting a captured body. New scheme binds timestamp into the signed input (Stripe-style). No legacy mode ‚Äî every outbound delivery carries a fresh sig so the cut is clean. Commit baecdd2.

- [x] SEC-L17. Cloudflare DNS retry backoff in `services/cloudflareDns.ts:91` now multiplies the deterministic delay (Retry-After or `base * 2^attempt`) by a random factor in [0.75, 1.25]. Prior purely-exponential backoff caused signup-burst clients to re-fire in lock-step and re-trigger the same 429. Jitter spreads retries across the backoff window. Commit 41657ff.

- [x] SEC-L32. `settings.routes.ts:1860` API-key `bcrypt.hashSync(rawKey, 10)` bumped to cost `12`. API keys carry full tenant scope and skip 2FA ‚Äî at cost 10 (~0.1s/attempt, Node default) the offline brute-force ceiling is 4√ó weaker than at 12 (~0.4s). Call is once per key creation so user-visible cost is negligible. Commit b62fb4d.

- [x] SEC-L21. `/reports/dashboard` cache key at `reports.routes.ts:34` now `dashboard:${tenantSlug}:${role}` ‚Äî was `dashboard:${tenantSlug}` only. Admin-first-hit no longer poisons the cashier response for the TTL window if any dashboard field is role-gated. Three cache buckets at most (admin/manager/technician) in a typical tenant; acceptable over-cache vs per-user explosion. Commit ea3085a.

- [x] SEC-L20. `catalogScraper.fetchSearchPage` in `services/catalogScraper.ts:390` now caps response body at 10 MiB before `cheerio.load(html)`. Layer 1: reject on `Content-Length > 10 MiB` pre-download. Layer 2: stream-read via `arrayBuffer()` and abort on `byteLength > 10 MiB`. Prior behavior fed arbitrary-size HTML into a synchronous parser, pinning the event loop and ballooning process memory on a malicious / runaway supplier page. Commit f49d746.

- [x] SEC-L19. Backup disk-space pre-check in `services/backup.ts:291` now requires 2√ó (dbSize + uploadsSize) free ‚Äî prior check only sized the DB. New helper `getDirectorySize()` walks `config.uploadsPath` silently; on sizing failure we fall back to dbSize-only (strictly safer than skipping). Error message splits the estimate so operators can see whether DB or uploads is the bigger consumer. Commit b005bf6.

- [x] SEC-L16. `getOrCreateWebhookSecret` in `services/webhooks.ts:56` rewritten to a race-safe `INSERT OR IGNORE ... VALUES ('webhook_secret', ?)` followed by a SELECT. Prior read ‚Üí branch ‚Üí INSERT-or-UPDATE let two concurrent first-time deliveries both generate their own 32-byte secret and race the PRIMARY KEY; loser's outbound payload was already signed with an orphan key the receiver couldn't verify. Atomic now. Commit e1f9591.

- [x] CROSS3. "Service" type tab removed from the inventory filter list on both surfaces. Android `InventoryListScreen.kt:158` `types` list is now `listOf("All", "Product", "Part")`. Web `InventoryListPage.tsx:10` `TABS` array drops the `{ key: 'service', label: 'Services' }` entry, and `InventoryCreatePage.tsx:92` removes the `<option value="service">Service</option>` from the item_type dropdown. Per scope, existing `inventory_items WHERE item_type='service'` rows are NOT migrated ‚Äî data migration is tracked separately ‚Äî and POS / ticket-wizard service pickers still resolve through the `repair_services` table, not inventory. Commit cf2eee0.

- [x] CROSS49. Initial-circle avatar now renders on `CustomerDetailScreen.kt` as the first row of the scrollable content (72dp `primaryContainer` background + `onPrimaryContainer` text, `headlineMedium` initial). The formerly-private `CustomerAvatar` composable in `CustomerListScreen.kt:264` was extracted to `ui/components/shared/CustomerAvatar.kt` with a `size: Dp` param so list (36dp) and detail (72dp) share one implementation. Orange-peach ramp is fine under the CROSS19 orange-primary theme. Commit 47374f9.

- [x] CROSS48. New `BrandPrimaryButton` / `BrandSecondaryButton` / `BrandTertiaryButton` composables in `ui/components/shared/BrandButtons.kt` lock in the canonical filled-vs-outlined-vs-text hierarchy: primary = `colorScheme.primary` fill + `onPrimary` text + `shapes.medium` (12dp), secondary = 1dp `primary` outline + `primary` text + 12dp shape, tertiary = `primary` text only. Adopted incrementally on the two most painful mismatches: `CustomerDetailScreen.kt` Call ‚Üí `BrandPrimaryButton`, SMS ‚Üí `BrandSecondaryButton`; `LoginScreen.kt` Sign-In ‚Üí `BrandPrimaryButton`. `BrandTextButton` kept as a deprecated alias routing to `BrandTertiaryButton` so existing call sites keep compiling. Remaining raw `Button { }` / `OutlinedButton { }` sites left for future incremental migration per scope. Commit e0ff700.

- [x] CROSS46. New `util/DateFormatter.kt` (extracted out of `util/Formatters.kt`) exposes two canonical APIs: `formatAbsolute(timestampMs: Long)` ‚Üí "April 16, 2026" (`LLLL d, yyyy`, locale default), `formatRelative(timestampMs: Long)` ‚Üí delegated to `android.text.format.DateUtils.getRelativeTimeSpanString` for "just now" / "5 min ago" / "in 2 hr". A companion `formatTimeOfDay(Long)` renders "h:mm a" for Settings-style "April 16, 2026 at 9:17 PM" rendering. Legacy String-based overloads (`formatDate`, `formatDateTime`, `formatRelative(String?)`, new `formatAbsolute(String?)`) preserved for existing call sites. Swept sites: Dashboard today-line (was `EEEE, MMMM d` ‚Üí `formatAbsolute(System.currentTimeMillis())`), AppointmentListScreen day header + DayHeader composable (was `EEEE, MMM d, yyyy` ‚Üí `formatAbsolute`), AppointmentCreateScreen `formatDisplayDate` (was `EEE, MMM d, yyyy` ‚Üí `formatAbsolute`), SettingsScreen `formatLastSync` (was custom `LLLL d 'at' h:mm a` ‚Üí composition of `formatRelative` for <1 day old and `formatAbsolute + formatTimeOfDay` beyond), TicketDetailScreen Created card (`formatDate` ‚Üí `formatAbsolute`), InvoiceDetailScreen Created line (was raw `createdAt.take(10)` ‚Üí `formatAbsolute`). CustomerDetailScreen doesn't currently render any date so no sweep site there. Commit bundled into 79773cc (carried along with the SEC-M33 migration commit due to a cross-session git interleave; content is correct).

- [x] CROSS45. `WaveDivider` placement unified to "directly below the TopAppBar / header row" on every list/dashboard screen: added to `InvoiceListScreen.kt`, `EstimateListScreen.kt`, `SmsListScreen.kt` (Messages ‚Äî previously had none), `LeadListScreen.kt`, `TicketListScreen.kt`, and `DashboardScreen.kt`. Each now wraps the TopAppBar in a `Column { BrandTopAppBar(...); WaveDivider() }` inside the `topBar` Scaffold slot. Existing sanctioned placements on LoginScreen (under wordmark), TicketSuccessScreen, SettingsScreen (above danger zone), and SharedComponents.EmptyState left untouched. Commit fc9178d.

- [x] SEC-M18. RMA + loaner list/detail GETs now gated on `requirePermission('inventory.adjust')`. Non-admin responses go through a `redactRmaForRole` / `redactLoanerForRole` helper that strips sensitive fields: RMA ‚Üí supplier_id/supplier_name/tracking_number/notes ‚Üí null; Loaner ‚Üí serial/imei ‚Üí null. Admin sees the full payload. Previously any authenticated user could scrape supplier relationships + shipment tracking numbers (RMA) or map hardware serials to customer names (loaners). Commit fe1e528.

- [x] SEC-M19. `/portal/embed/config` now (a) applies a 60-req / 5-min per-IP `consumeWindowRate` under the new `portal_embed_config` category (429 + Retry-After on over-limit), and (b) returns 404 unless the tenant has opted in via `store_config.portal_embed_enabled = '1'`. Previously the route was wide open and unthrottled ‚Äî attackers could harvest store_name / phone / address / logo across the entire tenant fleet by rotating Host headers. 404 (not 403) when disabled to keep "tenant exists but widget off" indistinguishable from "tenant doesn't exist". Commit bcebe88.

- [x] SEC-M31. `forEachDbAsync` in `index.ts:178` now races every per-tenant callback against a 30s timeout via a `withTimeout` helper. A hung tenant (stuck query, locked WAL, unresponsive file handle) used to stall all subsequent cron work (retention sweeps, appointment reminders, notifications). On timeout the bad tenant's iteration is logged and skipped; the loop proceeds to the next tenant. Iteration remains sequential. Commit 517204e.

- [x] SEC-M27. New `trackInterval` retention cron added to `index.ts` (right after the tenant sweep block) that runs once per UTC day at 03:00 and purges from the MASTER DB: `master_audit_log` older than 730 days, `tenant_auth_events` older than 90 days, `security_alerts` older than 730 days (unacked) / 180 days (acked). Followed by `incremental_vacuum(100)` to return freed pages. Prior state: no retention ‚Üí these append-only tables grew unbounded (tenant_auth_events especially ‚Äî one row per 2FA prompt). Commit f25a1a2.

- [x] SEC-M33. Credit-note overflow `store_credit_transactions` row (`invoices.routes.ts:891`) now uses `reference_type = 'credit_note_overflow'` instead of the previous `'invoice'`. Reporting/reconciliation tools can now isolate overflow credits from ordinary invoice-to-credit moves. Schema column is free-text `TEXT` so no migration is needed; `reference_id` still points at the source invoice for traceability. Commit 091902b.

- [x] SEC-M23. `recordLockoutFailure` in `utils/rateLimiter.ts:98` rewritten as a single `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT(category, key) DO UPDATE SET count = count + 1` statement. Prior SELECT ‚Üí branch ‚Üí INSERT-or-UPDATE pattern raced on concurrent TOTP / login failures: two simultaneous failures could both see row=null and contend on the UNIQUE(category, key) constraint, or the separate UPDATE could lose an increment. Now atomic at the SQL level. Commit 40c6fba.

- [x] SEC-M24. `/auth/change-password` now records the new bcrypt hash into `password_history` and prunes old rows INSIDE the same `adb.transaction([...])` as the user UPDATE + sessions DELETE. Previously the history INSERT happened in a follow-up `adb.run()` call ‚Äî a mid-request crash rotated the password but left history missing, letting the user reuse the new password on next rotation and silently bypass the P2FA8 reuse check. Commit 5406ce0.

- [x] SEC-M30. Per-tenant SQLite `cache_size` dropped from `-64000` (64 MiB) to `-16000` (16 MiB) in `db/tenant-pool.ts:103`. With `MAX_POOL_SIZE=50` the page-cache ceiling goes from 3.2 GiB ‚Üí ~800 MiB; typical tenant DB (<200 MiB) fits its hot working set in 16 MiB so query latency should not shift. Commit cc5060a.

- [x] SEC-M29. `/health` + `/api/v1/health` now round-trip the master DB via `SELECT 1` and return 503 `{success:false, message:"db unreachable"}` on failure ‚Äî an LB can distinguish "process alive" from "process alive with dead DB handle" (disk full, file locked, pool wedged). `/api/v1/health/ready` additionally round-trips `PRAGMA user_version` on top of the existing `isReady` boot flag so post-boot DB degradation drains the instance instead of serving 500s; `schemaVersion` is now echoed for ops. Commit 1bf3ae5.

Single-tenant detail endpoint (`GET /super-admin/tenants/:id`) still carries `db_path` for ops tooling. Commit fac0432.

- [x] SEC-H22. `POST /inventory/:id/adjust-stock` (inventory.routes.ts:1076) now role-gates to admin/manager and the UPDATE uses a differential `in_stock = in_stock + ? WHERE id = ? AND in_stock + ? >= 0` + `changes === 0 ‚Üí 400 Insufficient stock`. Replaces the prior read-check-write race where two parallel `-5` adjustments could both pass the JS precheck. Commit 50a1889.

- [x] SEC-H23. `DELETE /customers/:id` (customers.routes.ts:1222) now requires admin/manager role AND `body.confirm_name` exactly matching `first_name + ' ' + last_name`. - [x] SEC-H26. `POST /invoices/:id/payments` (invoices.routes.ts:377) now rejects with 400 when the request body includes a `customer_id` that does not match `invoice.customer_id`. Body value is validated as a positive integer first. Blocks UI bugs / forged requests that would post a payment against invoice A while declaring customer B (wrong ledger credit). - [x] SEC-H28. `PATCH /refunds/:id/approve` (refunds.routes.ts:165) now wraps the refund status flip + invoice amount_paid decrement in a single `adb.transaction([...])` with `expectChanges: true`. The refund UPDATE carries `WHERE id = ? AND status = 'pending'`; the invoice UPDATE carries `WHERE id = ? AND amount_paid = ?` with the snapshotted prior value. Either guard failing rolls the whole tx back and surfaces a 409. Commission-reversal + store-credit hooks remain post-tx (intentionally best-effort). Commit cb7f2b3.

- [x] SEC-H29. `POST /refunds` (refunds.routes.ts:79) now mounts the shared `idempotent` middleware (short-circuits double-submit within 5 min when `X-Idempotency-Key` is supplied) AND rejects with 403 unless the caller's role is admin or manager. Prevents cashier-tier rubber-stamp requests and the "user clicked Create twice ‚Üí two pending refund rows" failure mode. Commit bf43cf6.

- [x] SEC-H30. `PATCH /trade-ins/:id` (tradeIns.routes.ts:104) now requires admin/manager role when the requested status is `accepted`, and rejects any `accepted_price` that is not `Number.isFinite && > 0 && <= 100000` (even on non-accepting PATCHes so the field can never be pre-set absurdly low/high). Cap comes from the spec's sanity ceiling. Commit bf39cd2.

- [x] SEC-H31. `POST /rma` (rma.routes.ts:88) and `PATCH /rma/:id/status` (rma.routes.ts:133) both now mount `requirePermission('inventory.edit')`. RMA create/transition is an inventory/supplier-side action, so `inventory.edit` is the closest permission (no dedicated RMA key in PERMISSIONS). - [x] CROSS18. Root cause was the outer `Scaffold` in `AppNavGraph.kt` passing a `contentWindowInsets` whose top equals the system status bar height. Every child screen's own `Scaffold { topBar = BrandTopAppBar(...) }` also applies the status bar inset inside its `TopAppBar.windowInsets`, so the two stacked ‚Äî hence the ~200px of dead space above "New ticket" / "Dashboard" / "Customers" / "Messages". Fix: `contentWindowInsets = WindowInsets.systemBars.only(Horizontal + Bottom)` on the outer Scaffold so the top inset is owned exclusively by each screen's BrandTopAppBar. TicketCreate/Dashboard/CustomerList/SmsList bodies were already clean (no spurious `padding(top=‚Ä¶)`), so no per-screen edits required.
