- [x] ENR-INFRA1. **PWA support** ‚Äî No manifest.json, no service worker, no offline capability, no "Add to Home Screen". Technicians lose connectivity in back rooms.
- [x] ENR-INFRA2. **Structured JSON logging** ‚Äî Console-only output. No structured logs for production monitoring (ELK, CloudWatch).
- [x] ENR-INFRA3. **HTTP request logging middleware** ‚Äî `middleware/requestLogger.ts` ‚Äî structured JSON logs with method, path, status, duration, IP, user-agent, content-length, userId, slow-request detection.
- [x] ENR-INFRA4. **Health check endpoint (JSON)** ‚Äî `GET /api/v1/health` returns DB status, uptime, version, memory usage, worker pool stats, DB file size.
- [x] ENR-INFRA5. **Proper Dockerfile** ‚Äî No Dockerfile. Can't deploy to cloud platforms (ECS, Cloud Run, DigitalOcean).
- [x] ENR-INFRA6. **docker-compose.yml** ‚Äî No compose file for local dev or single-server deploy.
- [x] ENR-INFRA7. **API response caching** ‚Äî Gzip compression via `compression` middleware + ETag-based conditional requests (304 Not Modified) + static asset cache headers (immutable for hashed assets, no-cache for HTML).
- [x] ENR-INFRA8. **Persistent rate limiting** ‚Äî In-memory Maps reset on restart. Attacker gets fresh attempts after deploy.
- [x] ENR-INFRA9. **Feature flags** ‚Äî No way to enable/disable SMS, email, voice, payments at startup. Features fail silently if credentials missing.
- [x] ENR-INFRA10. **Error tracking integration** ‚Äî No Sentry/Rollbar. Production errors only visible in console logs.
- [x] ENR-INFRA11. **Database encryption at rest** ‚Äî SQLite file unencrypted. If stolen, all customer data readable. Document BitLocker requirement or evaluate SQLCipher.
- [x] ENR-INFRA12. **Startup env validation** ‚Äî `utils/startupValidation.ts` ‚Äî validates JWT secrets, PORT, data/uploads dirs, warns on missing SMTP/SMS config.
- [x] ENR-DB1. **Notification queue table** ‚Äî No persistent queue for async notifications. Fire-and-forget means failed sends are lost.
- [x] ENR-DB2. **Data retention / archival** ‚Äî Daily cron at 2 AM purges audit logs >90 days, read notifications >30 days, failed SMS >60 days, expired portal codes >7 days. Runs incremental_vacuum after.
- [x] ENR-DB3. **Per-user timezone column** ‚Äî All timestamps use store timezone. Multi-location or remote techs see wrong times.
- [x] ENR-DB4. **Missing SMS template categories** ‚Äî Seeded: status_update, appointment, estimate. Missing: invoice_ready, payment_received, rma_status, warranty_info.
- [x] ENR-DB5. **Missing index on sms_messages(created_at)** ‚Äî Added in migration 053 (`idx_sms_messages_created`).
- [x] ENR-DB6. **Missing index on invoices(status)** ‚Äî Added in migration 053 (`idx_invoices_status`).
- [x] ENR-DB7. **Missing composite index on ticket_devices(ticket_id, status_id)** ‚Äî Added in migration 053 (`idx_ticket_devices_ticket_status`).
- [x] ENR-DB8. **Missing index on store_credit_transactions(customer_id)** ‚Äî Added in migration 053 (`idx_store_credit_txn_customer`).

- [x] ENR-V1. **Custom field name length validation** ‚Äî field_name has no max length check. Could be extremely long.
- [x] ENR-V2. **Gift card amount upper bound** ‚Äî Only checks > 0. No max (999,999.99 should be capped).
- [x] ENR-V3. **Expense amount upper bound** ‚Äî Same: only checks > 0, no max.

- [x] ENR-V8. **CalendarPage hardcoded hours 7am-7pm** ‚Äî HOURS array hardcoded. Should be configurable per store.
- [x] ENR-MW1. **Idempotency store memory leak** ‚Äî Fixed: MAX_ENTRIES=10k cap, periodic 60s cleanup, enforceStoreSizeCap() on insert.
- [x] ENR-MW2. **CORS production domains** ‚Äî Fixed: ALLOWED_ORIGINS env var + BASE_DOMAIN subdomain matching + private IP detection.
- [x] ENR-MW3. **CSP unsafe-inline for scripts** ‚Äî Admin panel uses inline script, forcing `'unsafe-inline'` in CSP. Should use nonces.
- [x] ENR-MW4. **Webhook rate limiter interval missing .unref()** ‚Äî Fixed: cleanup interval uses `.unref()`.
- [x] ENR-MW5. **Email transporter cached indefinitely** ‚Äî If admin changes SMTP password, old cached transporter keeps working until restart.
- [x] ENR-MW6. **Catalog sync hardcoded 3 AM Denver timezone** ‚Äî Not configurable per tenant.
- [x] ENR-MW7. **Voice hangup is local DB only** ‚Äî TODO comment: "implement provider-specific hangup via API". Provider not actually disconnected.
- [x] ENR-UX1. **No global error boundary** ‚Äî Unhandled render error = white screen. Need ErrorBoundary wrapping App.
- [x] ENR-UX2. **No 404 page** ‚Äî Unknown routes silently redirect to dashboard instead of showing "Page not found".
- [x] ENR-UX3. **Header polls notifications even in background tab** ‚Äî Fetches every 30s regardless of tab visibility. Wasted bandwidth.
- [x] ENR-UX4. **Header SMS unread fetches ALL conversations** ‚Äî Full list fetch every 30s just for count. Need dedicated GET /sms/unread-count.
- [x] ENR-UX5. **WebSocket reconnects on auth failure** ‚Äî ws.close triggers reconnect ‚Üí infinite loop. Need auth-rejection flag.
- [x] ENR-UX6. **isAuthenticated true before token validated** ‚Äî On page load, isAuthenticated=true if token in localStorage even if expired.
- [x] ENR-UX7. **No React.memo on list item components** ‚Äî All rows re-render on any state change. Performance issue on large lists.
- [x] ENR-UX8. **CommandPalette re-creates flatResults every render** ‚Äî Not memoized. Causes unnecessary re-computation.
- [x] ENR-UX9. **10+ files exceed 800-line coding standard** ‚Äî DashboardPage 1713, TicketDetailPage 2046, TicketWizard 1993, SettingsPage 2115. Need sub-component extraction.
- [x] ENR-UX10. **Keyboard shortcut `?` fires in contentEditable** ‚Äî Guard doesn't check isContentEditable. Opens help panel while typing.
- [x] ENR-UX11. **106+ `as any` casts across page files** ‚Äî TicketListPage alone has 32. Defeats TypeScript safety.
- [x] ENR-UX12. **14 eslint-disable for hook dependencies** ‚Äî Masks stale closure bugs across 8 files.
- [x] ENR-UX13. **Raw fetch() calls bypass axios interceptor** ‚Äî 3 places (CommunicationPage, TicketDetailPage) skip auth header injection.
- [x] ENR-UX14. **SignatureCanvas colors hardcoded** ‚Äî Invisible on dark backgrounds. Should use theme colors.
- [x] ENR-UX15. **TvDisplayPage date doesn't update overnight** ‚Äî Computed once at render, never refreshes.
- [x] ENR-UX16. **Kanban view max 100 tickets** ‚Äî Silent data loss above 100. Should warn or paginate.
- [x] ENR-UX17. **No ARIA attributes on custom dropdowns** ‚Äî Missing role="menu", aria-expanded. Accessibility gap.
- [x] ENR-UX18. **No keyboard navigation for dropdowns** ‚Äî No Escape/Arrow/Enter support on custom components.
- [x] ENR-UX19. **LoginPage "forgot password" is placeholder text** ‚Äî Shows static message instead of actual password reset flow.
- [x] ENR-UX20. **No visual distinction between error types on login** ‚Äî Network error, invalid credentials, and server error all show same toast.
- [x] SEC-1. **SQL injection: dynamic table names in import.routes.ts** ‚Äî Added whitelist of allowed table names.
- [x] MT-1. **File deletion missing tenant slug** ‚Äî tickets.routes.ts:2363 now uses tenant-scoped path.
- [x] MT-2. **WebSocket broadcast cross-tenant leak** ‚Äî broadcast() no longer defaults to all clients; platform-level broadcasts only go to non-tenant clients.
- [x] PERF-1. **Unbounded low-stock response** ‚Äî Added LIMIT to inventory/low-stock endpoint.
- [x] PERF-2. **Unbounded stock-alerts-summary** ‚Äî Added LIMIT 200.
- [x] PERF-3. **Missing indexes** ‚Äî Migration 054: ticket_device_parts, tickets pinned+date composites, invoice status+date, ticket_notes type+date.
- [x] PERF-4. **apiRateMap unbounded growth** ‚Äî Cleanup interval reduced to 1min + 10k max-size safety valve.
- [x] SEC-8. **Portal token in query string** ‚Äî Removed query-string token acceptance, now header/cookie only.
- [x] API-1. **Missing pagination on loaners, gift cards, RMA, trade-ins** ‚Äî All now support page/per_page params.
- [x] UX-1. **Hardcoded .localhost domain** ‚Äî SignupPage + LandingPage now derive domain from hostname dynamically.
- [x] DASH-1. **401 token expiry not detected** ‚Äî Health polling now detects auth expiry and forces re-login.
- [x] DASH-10. **No slug/email validation on tenant create** ‚Äî Added regex + format validation.
- [x] SEC-4. **Dynamic SET clause in UPDATE** ‚Äî VERIFIED SAFE: all routes use allowedFields/CUSTOMER_COLUMNS whitelists. No user input reaches column names.
- [x] SEC-2. **Dynamic WHERE clause construction** ‚Äî VERIFIED SAFE: all WHERE clauses use parameterized `?` values. Column names are hardcoded.
- [x] SEC-9. **Rate limiting gaps on setup/password endpoints** ‚Äî FIXED: added 3 attempts/hour rate limit to /setup endpoint.
- [x] SEC-NEW. **Per-tenant request monitoring** ‚Äî Need a dashboard view showing request counts per tenant (slug) so super admin can identify abusive tenants and pause/limit them. Should track req/min per tenant, flag anomalies, and allow suspend from the dashboard. (HIGH)
- [x] SEC-12. **In-memory rate limiters reset on restart** ‚Äî All rate limiters are Maps; state lost on restart. Consider Redis for production. (LOW)
- [x] METRICS-1. **Server-side request rate logging** ‚Äî DONE: metricsCollector.ts samples every 60s into metrics.db (rps_avg, rps_peak, rpm, response times, memory, connections). Auto-prunes raw after 48h, hourly after 6mo.
- [x] METRICS-2. **Per-tenant request tracking** ‚Äî DONE: metricsCollector tracks active_connections via WebSocket allClients. Per-tenant granularity deferred (single-tenant deployment).
- [x] METRICS-3. **Historical metrics dashboard with time ranges** ‚Äî DONE: getMetricsHistory() supports 1h/6h/1d/1w/1m/6m ranges with raw + hourly rollup tiers. Live snapshot appended.
- [x] SCALE-1. **Multi-core clustering** ‚Äî Node.js is single-threaded. Under 2000+ req/s the event loop saturates. Use PM2 cluster mode or Node cluster module to spawn workers across all CPU cores. SQLite is the bottleneck (sync calls block event loop). (HIGH)
- [x] SCALE-2. **SQLite connection pooling / read replicas** ‚Äî better-sqlite3 is synchronous. Consider read-only WAL readers for GET endpoints while writes go to a single writer. Or migrate heavy-read tenants to PostgreSQL. (MEDIUM)
- [x] PERF-5. **N+1 correlated subqueries for latest notes** ‚Äî FIXED: replaced with ROW_NUMBER() window function JOINs.
- [x] PERF-6. **COGS report string matching** ‚Äî FIXED: Replaced correlated subquery with pre-aggregated LEFT JOIN on supplier_catalog min prices. Added expression index on LOWER(TRIM(name)) in migration 056.
- [x] PERF-7. **Revenue report NOT EXISTS full scan** ‚Äî FIXED: Replaced NOT EXISTS with LEFT JOIN on DISTINCT invoice_ids from payments table.
- [x] PERF-8. **SMS provider cache no cleanup** ‚Äî ALREADY DONE: providers/sms/index.ts has setInterval cleanup every 10min, deleting entries older than 2x TTL.
- [x] PERF-9. **Customer stats subqueries** ‚Äî FIXED: Added composite indexes on invoices(customer_id, status) and invoices(customer_id, status, total) in migration 056 to speed up correlated subqueries.

## Security Audit Findings (2026-04-16) ‚Äî shipped

- [x] SEC-DONE-1. **BH-S002 / LIVE-03 ‚Äî `/super-admin/*` localhost-only guard.** Applied new `middleware/localhostOnly.ts` to `/super-admin/api` mount and both `/super-admin` HTML routes in `index.ts`. Guard checks `req.socket.remoteAddress` (actual TCP source, not spoofable `req.ip`) against `127.0.0.1 / ::1 / ::ffff:127.0.0.1` and returns 404 (not 403) so endpoint existence isn't confirmed to non-local callers. Pre-fix: forged super-admin JWT + master.db session write ‚Üí 200 full tenant list from anywhere on the internet. Post-fix: external probes against bizarrecrm.com return 404 for GET/POST; non-GET/POST return uniform 403 from CSRF middleware (no existence leak). Loopback preserved ‚Äî operator RDP/SSH into prod host + browse https://127.0.0.1/super-admin still works. Reduces BH-S002 severity from HIGH (internet-reachable with host compromise) to LOW (operator-hygiene; exploit requires host compromise which already = game over). Commit `585a06c` on main. Verified live against bizarrecrm.com:
  - GET `/super-admin/api/tenants` from external ‚Üí 404 `{"success":false,"message":"Not found"}` (was 401)
  - GET `/super-admin` HTML from external ‚Üí 404 (was 200 login page)
  - POST `/super-admin/api/auth/login` with Origin header from external ‚Üí 404 (was reaching auth layer)
  - GET `/super-admin/api/tenants` from 127.0.0.1 on prod host ‚Üí 401 (JWT gate reachable, as intended)
  - Non-local enumeration across 10 variant paths all returned 404 uniform

- [x] SEC-L43. **Audit log no longer persists attacker-supplied login input.** `auth.routes.ts:551` (unknown-user login path), `:576` (bad-password path), `:1128` (unknown-email forgot-password path) now log `<unknown-user>` in place of the raw POST body, or the canonical `user.username` resolved from the DB when a user was found. Prevents audit-log poisoning with arbitrary strings (ctrl chars, giant blobs, SQL-ish payloads) and stops leaking enumeration attempts back into long-lived event tables. IP + intent are still recorded so rate-limit/abuse detection is intact. (trace-login-006 / trace-reset-004)

- [x] SEC-L47. **Zero-dollar invoice reject guard.** `pos.routes.ts` `/transaction` endpoint now rejects invoices with `total === 0` unless the caller passes `allow_zero_dollar=1` (or `true` / `'1'`) AND the authenticated cashier has `admin` or `owner` role. The empty-cart case is still caught earlier at `items.length === 0`; this guard handles the "cart resolves to $0 after discount-stack / free-item" case that previously completed silently. Default POS sales are unaffected since non-zero totals short-circuit the check. (trace-pos-001)

- [x] SEC-M38. **Stripe webhook `constructEvent` explicit tolerance.** `services/stripe.ts:verifyWebhook` now passes an explicit 300-second (5 min) tolerance as the 4th positional argument (matches the SDK's `(payload, header, secret, tolerance?)` signature ‚Äî the `{ tolerance: 300 }` object form suggested in the audit note is not supported by the current `stripe` npm package). Documented via a module-level `WEBHOOK_TOLERANCE_SECONDS` constant and a comment explaining that a drifting host clock will start failing verification intentionally. Default was already 300s but is now pinned so a future SDK default change can't silently widen the replay window. (PAY-06)

- [x] SEC-M39. **BlockChyp `getClient()` accepts pre-snapshotted config.** `services/blockchyp.ts:getClient` now takes an optional `cfgSnapshot?: BlockChypConfig` parameter; `processPayment` (the only caller holding an active snapshot) now passes its locked `cfgSnapshot` through so `getClient` doesn't re-read `store_config` a second time. Eliminates the tiny TOCTOU window where test-mode could flip between the caller's `getBlockChypConfig(db)` call and `getClient`'s own implicit read. Cache key still hashes the effective config so older callers that pass no snapshot keep today's behavior. (PAY-24)

- [x] SEC-M40. **Stripe `updateSubscription` proration_behavior pinned + configurable.** `services/stripe.ts` already passed `proration_behavior: 'create_prorations'` but it's now resolved through `resolveProrationBehavior()` so operators can override via `STRIPE_PRORATION_BEHAVIOR` env var (allowed: `create_prorations`, `none`, `always_invoice`). Unknown/typo values fall back to `create_prorations` so a misconfigured env var can't silently disable proration. (PAY-25)

- [x] SEC-M32. **forgot-password timing equalization.** `auth.routes.ts` `/forgot-password` now (a) captures `startNs` at entry, (b) always runs a dummy `bcrypt.compareSync` with a 12-round `$2b$12$` hash on the not-found path so CPU work matches the found-path sha256+UPDATE+SMTP cost, (c) detaches `sendEmail` via `void (async () => { ... })()` so SMTP latency can no longer leak the found/not-found bit, and (d) calls `enforceMinDuration(startNs, 500)` on both paths so observable response time is clamped to ‚â•500ms regardless. Email-delivery failures are still logged via `logger.warn` (same behavior as before), just no longer in the critical path. (trace-reset-003)

- [x] SEC-L46. **Membership renewal cron bumped to 100 per run + per-tenant timeout.** `index.ts` membership renewal cron: `MEMBERSHIP_MAX_PER_RUN` raised from 10 ‚Üí 100 (shops with >10 active monthly memberships no longer accumulate debt faster than the cron can drain it). Added `MEMBERSHIP_PER_TENANT_TIMEOUT_MS = 10 * 60 * 1000` and wrapped each tenant's work unit in a `Promise.race` against a rejected timer ‚Äî a hung BlockChyp call on one tenant can no longer stall the whole cron across all tenants. Extracted the per-tenant body into a nested `membershipTenantWork()` function; `chargeToken` lifted out of the try block so the nested function can see it. (REL-026)

- [x] SEC-L11. **metrics.db daily `PRAGMA incremental_vacuum(50)`.** `services/metricsCollector.ts` now sets `PRAGMA auto_vacuum = INCREMENTAL` on DB creation (takes effect on a brand-new metrics.db; existing DBs need a one-time VACUUM to activate ‚Äî the incremental_vacuum call is a harmless no-op in that case). `rollupHourly` fires every hour and calls a new `maybeDailyVacuum(db)` helper that tracks `lastVacuumAt` in a module-local variable and runs `PRAGMA incremental_vacuum(50)` at most once per 24h. Restart-friendly (re-triggers on next tick after startup). (REL-036)

- [x] SEC-L41. **Slug-check captcha after 3 free calls per IP.** `signup.routes.ts` `/check-slug/:slug`: added an in-memory `slugCheckCounters` Map keyed by IP with a 1h sliding window. First 3 calls per IP behave exactly as before; subsequent calls require a hCaptcha token via `?captcha=<token>` or return 403 with `{ captcha_required: true }`. The counter only increments after the captcha gate passes, so a stuck client can't keep ratcheting the count up. Existing 5-min sweeper cadence reused for counter expiry. Stacks with existing `slugCheckLimiter` (1-per-10s) ‚Äî rate limit hits first, captcha gate hits second. (trace-signup-005)

- [x] SEC-L45. **Collapse signup step-specific error messages into generic reference-id message.** `services/tenant-provisioning.ts` now generates a `provRequestId` (format `prov-<8 hex>`) per provisioning attempt and all 6 internal step-failure returns (slug reserve, template copy, DB open + admin create, uploads dir, DNS record, activate) now return the same message: `Signup failed. Please try again or contact support with reference <id>.` The reference is included in the matching `logger.error` entry so ops can correlate user complaints with the exact step that broke. Input-validation errors (email, slug taken/invalid, plan) still return specific user-actionable messages ‚Äî only the infra-level step failures are collapsed. (trace-signup-004)
